		private void tsbtnFindNoRangka_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
		{
			string query = "SELECT b.BatchNo, b.BatchInfo " +
				"FROM materialusageh AS muh " +
				"INNER JOIN materialusaged AS mud ON mud.DocNo=muh.DocNo " +
				"INNER JOIN batch AS b ON b.MaterialCode=mud.MaterialCode AND b.TagNo=mud.TagNo " +
				"WHERE muh.Status<>'DELETED' AND muh.JODocNo='" + txtJODocNo.Text + "' " +
				"ORDER BY b.BatchNo ";
				
			DataTable tbl = sql.Select(query);
			
			SIM.FrmGrid frmNoRangka = new SIM.FrmGrid("No Rangka", tbl);
			frmNoRangka.ShowDialog();
			
			if (frmNoRangka.ExDataRow != null)
			{
				frm.gcxDetail.ExGridView.SetFocusedRowCellValue("BatchNo", frmNoRangka.ExDataRow["BatchNo"].ToString());
				frm.gcxDetail.ExGridView.SetFocusedRowCellValue("BatchInfo", frmNoRangka.ExDataRow["BatchInfo"].ToString());
			}
		}

		private void BtnFill_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
		  if (this.txtmaterialusagehnotransfer.Text.ToString()!="") 	 
			{
				string query = "SELECT std.MaterialCode AS Code, mm.Name,std.TagNo,bc.BatchInfo,bc.ExpiryDate,std.Unit,std.qty,std.BaseQty " +
                "FROM stocktransferd as std " +
                "LEFT JOIN batch as bc on bc.Tagno=std.Tagno and bc.MaterialCode=std.MaterialCode " +
                "INNER JOIN MasterMaterial as mm on mm.Code = std.MaterialCode " +
				"INNER JOIN stocktransferh as sth on sth.docno = std.docno " +
                "WHERE sth.docno='" + txtmaterialusagehnotransfer.Text + "' and "+
				" sth.tolocation = '"+txtLocation.Text+"'";
				frm.tblDetail.Rows.Clear();
				frm.tblDetail.AcceptChanges();
				DataTable tblTemp = DB.sql.Select(query);
				int  rowcount = tblTemp.Rows.Count;
				frm.tblDetail.Merge(tblTemp);
				frm.tblDetail.AcceptChanges();
				if (rowcount == 0)
				{
					MessageBox.Show("Data Lokasi Pemakaian Produksi tidak sama dengan lokasi Tujuan Stock Transfer", "Errror", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
				}
				else
				{
                    this.txtJODocNo.Enabled = false;
				}
            }    
			
		}

        public bool OnBeforeSave()
		{
            if (txtmaterialusagehnotransfer.Text != "")
            {
                String query = "SELECT znojob from stocktransferh WHERE docno='" + txtmaterialusagehnotransfer.Text + "'";
                String TNohasil = DB.sql.SelectSingle(query, "").ToString();
                if (TNohasil != txtJODocNo.Text)
                {
                    MessageBox.Show("No Job Order tidak sesuai dengan data job order di transfer gudang", "Error", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
                    return false;
                }
                else return true;
            }
            else return true;              
		}

		private void tsbtnFindNoRangka_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
		{
			string query = "SELECT b.BatchNo, b.BatchInfo " +
				"FROM materialusageh AS muh " +
				"INNER JOIN materialusaged AS mud ON mud.DocNo=muh.DocNo " +
				"INNER JOIN batch AS b ON b.MaterialCode=mud.MaterialCode AND b.TagNo=mud.TagNo " +
				"WHERE muh.Status<>'DELETED' AND muh.JODocNo='" + txtJODocNo.Text + "' " +
				"ORDER BY b.BatchNo ";
				
			DataTable tbl = sql.Select(query);
			
			SIM.FrmGrid frmNoRangka = new SIM.FrmGrid("No Rangka", tbl);
			frmNoRangka.ShowDialog();
			
			if (frmNoRangka.ExDataRow != null)
			{
				frm.gcxDetail.ExGridView.SetFocusedRowCellValue("BatchNo", frmNoRangka.ExDataRow["BatchNo"].ToString());
				frm.gcxDetail.ExGridView.SetFocusedRowCellValue("BatchInfo", frmNoRangka.ExDataRow["BatchInfo"].ToString());
			}
		}

		private void BtnFill_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
			  string query = "SELECT std.MaterialCode AS Code, mm.Name,std.TagNo,bc.BatchInfo,bc.ExpiryDate,std.Unit,std.qty,std.BaseQty " +
                "FROM stocktransferd as std " +
                "LEFT JOIN batch as bc on bc.Tagno=std.Tagno and bc.MaterialCode=std.MaterialCode " +
                "INNER JOIN MasterMaterial as mm on mm.Code = std.MaterialCode " +
				"INNER JOIN stocktransferh as sth on sth.docno = std.docno " +
                "WHERE sth.docno='" + txtmaterialusagehnotransfer.Text + "' and "+
				" sth.tolocation = '"+txtLocation.Text+"'";
            frm.tblDetail.Rows.Clear();
            frm.tblDetail.AcceptChanges();
            DataTable tblTemp = DB.sql.Select(query);
            int  rowcount = tblTemp.Rows.Count;
            frm.tblDetail.Merge(tblTemp);
            frm.tblDetail.AcceptChanges();
            if (rowcount == 0)
            {
                MessageBox.Show("Data Lokasi Pemakaian Produksi tidak sama dengan lokasi Tujuan Stock Transfer", "Errror", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
            }
                
		}

        public bool OnBeforeSave()
		{
            if (txtmaterialusagehnotransfer.Text != "")
            {
                String query = "SELECT znojob from stocktransferh WHERE docno='" + txtmaterialusagehnotransfer.Text + "'";
                String TNohasil = DB.sql.SelectSingle(query, "").ToString();
                if (TNohasil != txtJODocNo.Text)
                {
                    MessageBox.Show("No Job Order tidak sesuai dengan data job order di transfer gudang", "Error", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
                    return false;
                }
                else return true;
            }
            else return true;              
		}

		private void BtnFill_Click(object sender, EventArgs e)
        {
		  if (this.txtmaterialusagehnotransfer.Text.ToString()=="") 	 
			{
				string query = "SELECT std.MaterialCode AS Code, mm.Name,std.TagNo,bc.BatchInfo,bc.ExpiryDate,std.Unit,std.qty,std.BaseQty " +
                "FROM stocktransferd as std " +
                "LEFT JOIN batch as bc on bc.Tagno=std.Tagno and bc.MaterialCode=std.MaterialCode " +
                "INNER JOIN MasterMaterial as mm on mm.Code = std.MaterialCode " +
				"INNER JOIN stocktransferh as sth on sth.docno = std.docno " +
                "WHERE sth.docno='" + txtmaterialusagehnotransfer.Text + "' and "+
				" sth.tolocation = '"+txtLocation.Text+"'";
				frm.tblDetail.Rows.Clear();
				frm.tblDetail.AcceptChanges();
				DataTable tblTemp = DB.sql.Select(query);
				int  rowcount = tblTemp.Rows.Count;
				frm.tblDetail.Merge(tblTemp);
				frm.tblDetail.AcceptChanges();
				if (rowcount == 0)
				{
					MessageBox.Show("Data Lokasi Pemakaian Produksi tidak sama dengan lokasi Tujuan Stock Transfer", "Errror", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
				}
				else
				{
                    this.txtJODocNo.Enabled = false;
				}
            }    
			
		}

        public bool OnBeforeSave()
		{
            if (txtmaterialusagehnotransfer.Text != "")
            {
                String query = "SELECT znojob from stocktransferh WHERE docno='" + txtmaterialusagehnotransfer.Text + "'";
                String TNohasil = DB.sql.SelectSingle(query, "").ToString();
                if (TNohasil != txtJODocNo.Text)
                {
                    MessageBox.Show("No Job Order tidak sesuai dengan data job order di transfer gudang", "Error", MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
                    return false;
                }
                else return true;
            }
            else return true;              
		}

            if (e.RowHandle < 0) return; //Skip new row or filter row

            if (e.Column.Name == "colQty" || e.Column.Name == "colPrice")
            {
                tblDetail.AcceptChanges();
                foreach(DataRow row in tblDetail.Rows)
                {
                    row["Total"] = decimal.Parse(row["Qty"].ToString()) * decimal.Parse(row["Price"].ToString());
                }    
            }
        }
        */
	}
}, CreatedBy: admin, CreatedDate: 2023-06-20T09:33:38

  - NAME: CreatedBy, TYPE: varchar(16), NULLABLE: NO, KEY: , DEFAULT: None, EXTRA: , COMMENT: 
  - NAME: CreatedDate, TYPE: datetime, NULLABLE: NO, KEY: , DEFAULT: None, EXTRA: , COMMENT: 
  - NAME: ChangedBy, TYPE: varchar(16), NULLABLE: NO, KEY: , DEFAULT: None, EXTRA: , COMMENT:

SAMPLE_DATA (LIMIT 3):
  - Name: cubepointofsale, Description: Cube Point Of Sale, Query: SELECT DATE_ADD(posh.DocDate,INTERVAL DAY(posh.DocDate)*-1 + 1 DAY) AS DocDate, posh.Series, posh.Location, posh.SalesCode, posh.CustomerCode, posd.MaterialCode,
  (CASE WHEN poh.DocNo IS NOT NULL THEN grh.SupplierCode ELSE (SELECT IFNULL(MAX(SupplierCode),'') FROM mastermaterials AS mms WHERE mms.Code=posd.MaterialCode ORDER BY mms.Priority LIMIT 1) END) AS SupplierCode,
	SUM(posd.BaseQty) AS BaseQty, SUM(posd.Netto) AS Netto, SUM(posd.Cost) AS Cost,
	SUM(posd.DiscNominal + (posd.Netto * posh.DiscPercent / 100)) AS DiscNominalAndHeaderDisc,
	SUM(posd.Netto - (posd.Netto * posh.DiscPercent / 100)) AS NettoAfterHeaderDisc
FROM pointofsaleh AS posh
INNER JOIN pointofsaled AS posd ON posh.DocNo=posd.DocNo
LEFT JOIN goodsreceiptd AS grd ON grd.MaterialCode=posd.MaterialCode AND grd.TagNo=posd.TagNo
LEFT JOIN goodsreceipth AS grh ON grh.DocNo=grd.DocNo
LEFT JOIN purchaseorderh AS poh ON poh.DocNo=grh.PODocNo AND poh.Series IN (SELECT Series FROM masterdocumentseries WHERE Document='PURCHASE ORDER')
WHERE posh.Status <> 'DELETED' AND posh.DocDate BETWEEN #StartDate# AND #EndDate#
GROUP BY DocDate, posh.Series, posh.Location, posh.SalesCode, posh.CustomerCode, posd.MaterialCode, grh.SupplierCode, CreatedBy: root, CreatedDate: 2023-12-05T07:57:56, ChangedBy: root, ChangedDate: 2023-12-05T07:57:56
---
